         <a class="tout-title-link" data-analytics-module="hero" data-analytics-position="1" href="/astrazenecas-covid-19-shot-trial-results-in-large-trial-2021-2">
          AstraZeneca's COVID-19 shot was 79% effective in a trial involving 32,000 people, paving the way for US authorization
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="tout-copy featured-tout typography">
         <ul>
          <li>
           A large US trial found the COVID-19 shot from AstraZeneca and Oxford University 79% effective.
          </li>
          <li>
           There was no evidence of blood clots in the US trial.
          </li>
          <li>
           The drugmaker can now submit data for scrutiny by the FDA, ahead of potential authorization.
          </li>
         </ul>
